\documentclass[11pt]{article}

    \usepackage[breakable]{tcolorbox}
    \usepackage{parskip} % Stop auto-indenting (to mimic markdown behaviour)
    

    % Basic figure setup, for now with no caption control since it's done
    % automatically by Pandoc (which extracts ![](path) syntax from Markdown).
    \usepackage{graphicx}
    % Keep aspect ratio if custom image width or height is specified
    \setkeys{Gin}{keepaspectratio}
    % Maintain compatibility with old templates. Remove in nbconvert 6.0
    \let\Oldincludegraphics\includegraphics
    % Ensure that by default, figures have no caption (until we provide a
    % proper Figure object with a Caption API and a way to capture that
    % in the conversion process - todo).
    \usepackage{caption}
    \DeclareCaptionFormat{nocaption}{}
    \captionsetup{format=nocaption,aboveskip=0pt,belowskip=0pt}

    \usepackage{float}
    \floatplacement{figure}{H} % forces figures to be placed at the correct location
    \usepackage{xcolor} % Allow colors to be defined
    \usepackage{enumerate} % Needed for markdown enumerations to work
    \usepackage{geometry} % Used to adjust the document margins
    \usepackage{amsmath} % Equations
    \usepackage{amssymb} % Equations
    \usepackage{textcomp} % defines textquotesingle
    % Hack from http://tex.stackexchange.com/a/47451/13684:
    \AtBeginDocument{%
        \def\PYZsq{\textquotesingle}% Upright quotes in Pygmentized code
    }
    \usepackage{upquote} % Upright quotes for verbatim code
    \usepackage{eurosym} % defines \euro

    \usepackage{iftex}
    \ifPDFTeX
        \usepackage[T1]{fontenc}
        \IfFileExists{alphabeta.sty}{
              \usepackage{alphabeta}
          }{
              \usepackage[mathletters]{ucs}
              \usepackage[utf8x]{inputenc}
          }
    \else
        \usepackage{fontspec}
        \usepackage{unicode-math}
    \fi

    \usepackage{fancyvrb} % verbatim replacement that allows latex
    \usepackage{grffile} % extends the file name processing of package graphics
                         % to support a larger range
    \makeatletter % fix for old versions of grffile with XeLaTeX
    \@ifpackagelater{grffile}{2019/11/01}
    {
      % Do nothing on new versions
    }
    {
      \def\Gread@@xetex#1{%
        \IfFileExists{"\Gin@base".bb}%
        {\Gread@eps{\Gin@base.bb}}%
        {\Gread@@xetex@aux#1}%
      }
    }
    \makeatother
    \usepackage[Export]{adjustbox} % Used to constrain images to a maximum size
    \adjustboxset{max size={0.9\linewidth}{0.9\paperheight}}

    % The hyperref package gives us a pdf with properly built
    % internal navigation ('pdf bookmarks' for the table of contents,
    % internal cross-reference links, web links for URLs, etc.)
    \usepackage{hyperref}
    % The default LaTeX title has an obnoxious amount of whitespace. By default,
    % titling removes some of it. It also provides customization options.
    \usepackage{titling}
    \usepackage{longtable} % longtable support required by pandoc >1.10
    \usepackage{booktabs}  % table support for pandoc > 1.12.2
    \usepackage{array}     % table support for pandoc >= 2.11.3
    \usepackage{calc}      % table minipage width calculation for pandoc >= 2.11.1
    \usepackage[inline]{enumitem} % IRkernel/repr support (it uses the enumerate* environment)
    \usepackage[normalem]{ulem} % ulem is needed to support strikethroughs (\sout)
                                % normalem makes italics be italics, not underlines
    \usepackage{soul}      % strikethrough (\st) support for pandoc >= 3.0.0
    \usepackage{mathrsfs}
    

    
    % Colors for the hyperref package
    \definecolor{urlcolor}{rgb}{0,.145,.698}
    \definecolor{linkcolor}{rgb}{.71,0.21,0.01}
    \definecolor{citecolor}{rgb}{.12,.54,.11}

    % ANSI colors
    \definecolor{ansi-black}{HTML}{3E424D}
    \definecolor{ansi-black-intense}{HTML}{282C36}
    \definecolor{ansi-red}{HTML}{E75C58}
    \definecolor{ansi-red-intense}{HTML}{B22B31}

    \definecolor{ansi-green-intense}{HTML}{007427}

    \definecolor{ansi-yellow-intense}{HTML}{B27D12}

    \definecolor{ansi-blue-intense}{HTML}{0065CA}
    \definecolor{ansi-magenta}{HTML}{D160C4}
    \definecolor{ansi-magenta-intense}{HTML}{A03196}

    \definecolor{ansi-cyan-intense}{HTML}{258F8F}
    \definecolor{ansi-white}{HTML}{C5C1B4}
    \definecolor{ansi-white-intense}{HTML}{A1A6B2}
    \definecolor{ansi-default-inverse-fg}{HTML}{FFFFFF}
    \definecolor{ansi-default-inverse-bg}{HTML}{000000}

    % common color for the border for error outputs.
    \definecolor{outerrorbackground}{HTML}{FFDFDF}

    % commands and environments needed by pandoc snippets
    % extracted from the output of `pandoc -s`
    \providecommand{\tightlist}{%
      \setlength{\itemsep}{0pt}\setlength{\parskip}{0pt}}
    \DefineVerbatimEnvironment{Highlighting}{Verbatim}{commandchars=\\\{\}}
    % Add ',fontsize=\small' for more characters per line
    \newenvironment{Shaded}{}{}
    \newcommand{\KeywordTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.00,0.44,0.13}{\textbf{{#1}}}}
    \newcommand{\DataTypeTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.56,0.13,0.00}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\DecValTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.25,0.63,0.44}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\BaseNTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.25,0.63,0.44}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\FloatTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.25,0.63,0.44}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\CharTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.25,0.44,0.63}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\StringTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.25,0.44,0.63}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\CommentTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.38,0.63,0.69}{\textit{{#1}}}}
    \newcommand{\OtherTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.00,0.44,0.13}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\AlertTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{1.00,0.00,0.00}{\textbf{{#1}}}}
    \newcommand{\FunctionTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.02,0.16,0.49}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\RegionMarkerTok}[1]{{#1}}
    \newcommand{\ErrorTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{1.00,0.00,0.00}{\textbf{{#1}}}}
    \newcommand{\NormalTok}[1]{{#1}}

    % Additional commands for more recent versions of Pandoc
    \newcommand{\ConstantTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.53,0.00,0.00}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\SpecialCharTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.25,0.44,0.63}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\VerbatimStringTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.25,0.44,0.63}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\SpecialStringTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.73,0.40,0.53}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\ImportTok}[1]{{#1}}
    \newcommand{\DocumentationTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.73,0.13,0.13}{\textit{{#1}}}}
    \newcommand{\AnnotationTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.38,0.63,0.69}{\textbf{\textit{{#1}}}}}
    \newcommand{\CommentVarTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.38,0.63,0.69}{\textbf{\textit{{#1}}}}}
    \newcommand{\VariableTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.10,0.09,0.49}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\ControlFlowTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.00,0.44,0.13}{\textbf{{#1}}}}
    \newcommand{\OperatorTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.40,0.40,0.40}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\BuiltInTok}[1]{{#1}}
    \newcommand{\ExtensionTok}[1]{{#1}}
    \newcommand{\PreprocessorTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.74,0.48,0.00}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\AttributeTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.49,0.56,0.16}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\InformationTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.38,0.63,0.69}{\textbf{\textit{{#1}}}}}
    \newcommand{\WarningTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.38,0.63,0.69}{\textbf{\textit{{#1}}}}}
    \makeatletter
    \newsavebox\pandoc@box
    \newcommand*\pandocbounded[1]{%
      \sbox\pandoc@box{#1}%
      % scaling factors for width and height
      \Gscale@div\@tempa\textheight{\dimexpr\ht\pandoc@box+\dp\pandoc@box\relax}%
      \Gscale@div\@tempb\linewidth{\wd\pandoc@box}%
      % select the smaller of both
      \ifdim\@tempb\p@<\@tempa\p@
        \let\@tempa\@tempb
      \fi
      % scaling accordingly (\@tempa < 1)
      \ifdim\@tempa\p@<\p@
        \scalebox{\@tempa}{\usebox\pandoc@box}%
      % scaling not needed, use as it is
      \else
        \usebox{\pandoc@box}%
      \fi
    }
    \makeatother

    % Define a nice break command that doesn't care if a line doesn't already
    % exist.
    \def\br{\hspace*{\fill} \\* }
    % Math Jax compatibility definitions
    \def\gt{>}
    \def\lt{<}
    \let\Oldtex\TeX
    \let\Oldlatex\LaTeX
    \renewcommand{\TeX}{\textrm{\Oldtex}}
    \renewcommand{\LaTeX}{\textrm{\Oldlatex}}
    % Document parameters
    % Document title
    \title{Air\_Quality\_Index\_Forecasting}
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
% Pygments definitions
\makeatletter
\def\PY@reset{\let\PY@it=\relax \let\PY@bf=\relax%
    \let\PY@ul=\relax \let\PY@tc=\relax%
    \let\PY@bc=\relax \let\PY@ff=\relax}
\def\PY@tok#1{\csname PY@tok@#1\endcsname}
\def\PY@toks#1+{\ifx\relax#1\empty\else%
    \PY@tok{#1}\expandafter\PY@toks\fi}
\def\PY@do#1{\PY@bc{\PY@tc{\PY@ul{%
    \PY@it{\PY@bf{\PY@ff{#1}}}}}}}
\def\PY#1#2{\PY@reset\PY@toks#1+\relax+\PY@do{#2}}

\def\PYZbs{\char`\\}
\def\PYZus{\char`\_}
\def\PYZob{\char`\{}
\def\PYZcb{\char`\}}
\def\PYZca{\char`\^}
\def\PYZam{\char`\&}
\def\PYZlt{\char`\<}
\def\PYZgt{\char`\>}
\def\PYZsh{\char`\#}
\def\PYZpc{\char`\%}
\def\PYZdl{\char`\$}

    % For linebreaks inside Verbatim environment from package fancyvrb.
    \makeatletter
        \newbox\Wrappedcontinuationbox
        \newbox\Wrappedvisiblespacebox
        \newcommand*\Wrappedvisiblespace {\textcolor{red}{\textvisiblespace}}
        \newcommand*\Wrappedcontinuationsymbol {\textcolor{red}{\llap{\tiny$\m@th\hookrightarrow$}}}
        \newcommand*\Wrappedcontinuationindent {3ex }
        \newcommand*\Wrappedafterbreak {\kern\Wrappedcontinuationindent\copy\Wrappedcontinuationbox}
        % Take advantage of the already applied Pygments mark-up to insert
        % potential linebreaks for TeX processing.
        %        {, <, #, %, $, ' and ": go to next line.
        %        _, }, ^, &, >, - and ~: stay at end of broken line.
        % Use of \textquotesingle for straight quote.
        \newcommand*\Wrappedbreaksatspecials {%
            \def\PYGZus{\discretionary{\char`\_}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\_}}%
            \def\PYGZob{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\{}{\char`\{}}%
            \def\PYGZcb{\discretionary{\char`\}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\}}}%
            \def\PYGZca{\discretionary{\char`\^}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\^}}%
            \def\PYGZam{\discretionary{\char`\&}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\&}}%
            \def\PYGZlt{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\<}{\char`\<}}%
            \def\PYGZgt{\discretionary{\char`\>}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\>}}%
            \def\PYGZsh{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\#}{\char`\#}}%
            \def\PYGZpc{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\%}{\char`\%}}%
            \def\PYGZdl{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\$}{\char`\$}}%
            \def\PYGZhy{\discretionary{\char`\-}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\-}}%
            \def\PYGZsq{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\textquotesingle}{\textquotesingle}}%
            \def\PYGZdq{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\"}{\char`\"}}%
            \def\PYGZti{\discretionary{\char`\~}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\~}}%
        }
        % Some characters . , ; ? ! / are not pygmentized.
        % This macro makes them "active" and they will insert potential linebreaks
        \newcommand*\Wrappedbreaksatpunct {%
            \lccode`\~`\.\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\.}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\.}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\,\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\,}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\,}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\;\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\;}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\;}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\:\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\:}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\:}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\?\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\?}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\?}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\!\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\!}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\!}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\/\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\/}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\/}}}%
            \catcode`\.\active
            \catcode`\,\active
            \catcode`\;\active
            \catcode`\:\active
            \catcode`\?\active
            \catcode`\!\active
            \catcode`\/\active
            \lccode`\~`\~
        }
    \makeatother

    \let\OriginalVerbatim=\Verbatim
    \makeatletter
    \renewcommand{\Verbatim}[1][1]{%
        %\parskip\z@skip
        \sbox\Wrappedcontinuationbox {\Wrappedcontinuationsymbol}%
        \sbox\Wrappedvisiblespacebox {\FV@SetupFont\Wrappedvisiblespace}%
        \def\FancyVerbFormatLine ##1{\hsize\linewidth
            \vtop{\raggedright\hyphenpenalty\z@\exhyphenpenalty\z@
                \doublehyphendemerits\z@\finalhyphendemerits\z@
                \strut ##1\strut}%
        }%
        % If the linebreak is at a space, the latter will be displayed as visible
        % space at end of first line, and a continuation symbol starts next line.
        % Stretch/shrink are however usually zero for typewriter font.
        \def\FV@Space {%
            \nobreak\hskip\z@ plus\fontdimen3\font minus\fontdimen4\font
            \discretionary{\copy\Wrappedvisiblespacebox}{\Wrappedafterbreak}
            {\kern\fontdimen2\font}%
        }%

        % Allow breaks at special characters using \PYG... macros.
        \Wrappedbreaksatspecials
        % Breaks at punctuation characters . , ; ? ! and / need catcode=\active
        \OriginalVerbatim[#1,codes*=\Wrappedbreaksatpunct]%
    }
    \makeatother

    % Exact colors from NB
    \definecolor{incolor}{HTML}{303F9F}
    \definecolor{outcolor}{HTML}{D84315}
    \definecolor{cellborder}{HTML}{CFCFCF}
    \definecolor{cellbackground}{HTML}{F7F7F7}

    % prompt
    \makeatletter
    \newcommand{\boxspacing}{\kern\kvtcb@left@rule\kern\kvtcb@boxsep}
    \makeatother
    \newcommand{\prompt}[4]{
        {\ttfamily\llap{{\color{#2}[#3]:\hspace{3pt}#4}}\vspace{-\baselineskip}}
    }
    

    
    % Prevent overflowing lines due to hard-to-break entities
    \sloppy
    % Setup hyperref package
    \hypersetup{
      breaklinks=true,  % so long urls are correctly broken across lines
      colorlinks=true,
      urlcolor=urlcolor,
      linkcolor=linkcolor,

\PY{k+kn}{from}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{statsmodels}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{tsa}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{stattools}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{adfuller}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Perform ADF test}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 1. McLeod\PYZhy{}Li Test for Nonlinearity (ARCH Test)}
\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{mcleod\PYZus{}li\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{model\PYZus{}null}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}

    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{McLeod\PYZhy{}Li (ARCH) Test p\PYZhy{}value: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{p\PYZus{}value}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 3. Tsay\PYZsq{}s Test for Nonlinearity (ADF test on residuals)}
\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{tsays\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{model\PYZus{}null}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{tsay\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}func}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{residuals}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}

    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{Tsay Test p\PYZhy{}value (ADF on residuals): }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{p\PYZus{}value\PYZus{}tsay}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{The test suggests nonlinearity in the residuals (structural break or nonstationarity).}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{No significant evidence of nonlinearity in the residuals.}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 4. Likelihood Ratio Test for Threshold Nonlinearity}
\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{likelihood\PYZus{}ratio\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{model\PYZus{}null}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Threshold}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Time}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{50}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{astype}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{)}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Define a threshold}
    \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}complex} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{sm}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{add\PYZus{}constant}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Time}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Threshold}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{model\PYZus{}complex} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{sm}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{OLS}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}complex}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{fit}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{n}{log\PYZus{}likelihood\PYZus{}null} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{model\PYZus{}null}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{llf}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Log\PYZhy{}likelihood of null model}
    \PY{n}{log\PYZus{}likelihood\PYZus{}complex} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{model\PYZus{}complex}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{llf}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Log\PYZhy{}likelihood of alternative model}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Likelihood Ratio Test}
    \PY{n}{lrt\PYZus{}statistic} \PY{o}{=} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{2} \PY{o}{*} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{log\PYZus{}likelihood\PYZus{}null} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{log\PYZus{}likelihood\PYZus{}complex}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{df} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{model\PYZus{}complex}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{params}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{model\PYZus{}null}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{params}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{p\PYZus{}value\PYZus{}lrt} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{chi2}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sf}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{lrt\PYZus{}statistic}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{Likelihood Ratio Test p\PYZhy{}value: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{p\PYZus{}value\PYZus{}lrt}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{p\PYZus{}value\PYZus{}lrt} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.05}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{The test suggests threshold nonlinearity (better fit with threshold model).}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{No significant evidence of threshold nonlinearity.}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 5. Teresvitas\PYZsq{} Neural Network Test for Nonlinearity}
\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{teresvitas\PYZus{}nn\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Standardize the data before feeding it to the neural network}
    \PY{n}{scaler} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{StandardScaler}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}scaled} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{scaler}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{fit\PYZus{}transform}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Time}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}scaled} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{AQI Index}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{values}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Define the model using Input layer}
    \PY{n}{nn\PYZus{}model} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Sequential}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{[}
        \PY{n}{Input}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Specify the input shape using Input layer}
        \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{10}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}
        \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{nn\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{compile}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{optimizer}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{adam}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{loss}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{mean\PYZus{}squared\PYZus{}error}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Train the neural network}
    \PY{n}{nn\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{fit}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}scaled}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}scaled}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{epochs}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{100}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{verbose}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Get predictions from the neural network}
    \PY{n}{nn\PYZus{}predictions} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{nn\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{predict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}scaled}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Compare with the linear model predictions}
    \PY{n}{linear\PYZus{}predictions} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{model\PYZus{}null}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{predict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Calculate the Mean Squared Error (MSE) of both models}
    \PY{n}{mse\PYZus{}nn} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{nn\PYZus{}predictions} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}scaled}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*}\PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{mse\PYZus{}linear} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{linear\PYZus{}predictions} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}scaled}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*}\PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{Teresvitas}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ Neural Network Test:}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Neural Network MSE: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{mse\PYZus{}nn}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{, Linear Model MSE: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{mse\PYZus{}linear}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{mse\PYZus{}nn} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{n}{mse\PYZus{}linear}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{The neural network model performs better, suggesting nonlinearity.}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{The linear model performs better, suggesting linearity.}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 6. White\PYZsq{}s Neural Network Test for Nonlinearity}
\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{whites\PYZus{}nn\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{model\PYZus{}null}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Standardize the data before feeding it to the neural network}
    \PY{n}{scaler} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{StandardScaler}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}scaled} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{scaler}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{fit\PYZus{}transform}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Time}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}scaled} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{AQI Index}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{values}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Define a neural network model}
    \PY{n}{nn\PYZus{}model} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Sequential}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{[}
        \PY{n}{Input}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Specify the input shape using Input layer}
        \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{10}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}
        \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{nn\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{compile}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{optimizer}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{adam}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{loss}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{mean\PYZus{}squared\PYZus{}error}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Train the neural network}
    \PY{n}{nn\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{fit}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}scaled}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}scaled}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{epochs}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{100}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{verbose}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Get predictions from the neural network}
    \PY{n}{nn\PYZus{}predictions} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{nn\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{predict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}scaled}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Calculate residuals from the linear model}
    \PY{n}{linear\PYZus{}predictions} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{model\PYZus{}null}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{predict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{residuals\PYZus{}linear} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}scaled} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{linear\PYZus{}predictions}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Calculate the MSE of the residuals from the neural network}
    \PY{n}{mse\PYZus{}nn} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{nn\PYZus{}predictions} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}scaled}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*}\PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{White}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{s Neural Network Test:}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Neural Network MSE on residuals: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{mse\PYZus{}nn}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{mse\PYZus{}nn} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{residuals\PYZus{}linear} \PY{o}{*}\PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{The neural network better fits the residuals, suggesting nonlinearity.}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{The linear model residuals are better, suggesting linearity.}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Run all tests}
\PY{n}{mcleod\PYZus{}li\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{model\PYZus{}null}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{kenans\PYZus{}reset\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{model\PYZus{}null}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{tsays\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{model\PYZus{}null}\PY{p}{)}

    \hypertarget{interpretation-of-nonlinearity-heteroscedasticity-tests}{%
\section{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{Interpretation of Nonlinearity \&
Heteroscedasticity
Tests}}{Interpretation of Nonlinearity \& Heteroscedasticity Tests}}\label{interpretation-of-nonlinearity-heteroscedasticity-tests}}

\hypertarget{mcleod-li-arch-test}{%
\subsection{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{➤ McLeod-Li (ARCH)
Test}}{➤ McLeod-Li (ARCH) Test}}\label{mcleod-li-arch-test}}

\textbf{p-value: 3.019 × 10⁻²⁶²} (Extremely low)\\
📌 \textbf{Interpretation:}\\
- Strong evidence of \textbf{heteroscedasticity} (variance changes over
time).\\
- The model may need \textbf{GARCH-type adjustments} to handle
volatility.

\begin{center}\rule{0.5\linewidth}{0.5pt}\end{center}

\hypertarget{kenans-reset-test}{%
\subsection{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{➤ Kenan's RESET
Test}}{➤ Kenan's RESET Test}}\label{kenans-reset-test}}

\textbf{p-value: 1.202 × 10⁻⁴¹} (Extremely low)\\
📌 \textbf{Interpretation:}\\
- Suggests \textbf{model misspecification} due to nonlinearity.\\
- Consider \textbf{higher-order polynomial terms} or \textbf{nonlinear
transformations}.

\begin{center}\rule{0.5\linewidth}{0.5pt}\end{center}

\hypertarget{tsay-test-adf-on-residuals}{%
\subsection{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{➤ Tsay Test (ADF on
Residuals)}}{➤ Tsay Test (ADF on Residuals)}}\label{tsay-test-adf-on-residuals}}

\textbf{p-value: 0.0009} (Very low)\\
📌 \textbf{Interpretation:}\\
- Indicates \textbf{nonlinearity in residuals}, possibly due to
\textbf{structural breaks} or \textbf{nonstationarity}.\\
- Differencing or \textbf{regime-switching models} may help improve
performance.

\begin{center}\rule{0.5\linewidth}{0.5pt}\end{center}

\hypertarget{likelihood-ratio-test}{%
\subsection{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{➤ Likelihood Ratio
Test}}{➤ Likelihood Ratio Test}}\label{likelihood-ratio-test}}

\textbf{p-value: 0.3507} (Not significant)\\
📌 \textbf{Interpretation:}\\
- No evidence of \textbf{threshold nonlinearity}.\\
- The model does not exhibit significant \textbf{regime shifts}.

\begin{center}\rule{0.5\linewidth}{0.5pt}\end{center}

\hypertarget{neural-network-based-linearity-tests}{%
\section{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{Neural Network-Based Linearity
Tests}}{Neural Network-Based Linearity Tests}}\label{neural-network-based-linearity-tests}}

\hypertarget{teresvitas-neural-network-test}{%
\subsection{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{➤ Teresvitas' Neural Network
Test}}{➤ Teresvitas' Neural Network Test}}\label{teresvitas-neural-network-test}}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  \textbf{Neural Network MSE:} \textbf{11325.17}\\
\item
  \textbf{Linear Model MSE:} \textbf{10987.98}\\
  📌 \textbf{Interpretation:}\\
\item
  The linear model \textbf{performs slightly better}, suggesting that a
  linear approach may be sufficient.\\
\item
  Nonlinear models may not provide significant improvements.
\end{itemize}

\begin{center}\rule{0.5\linewidth}{0.5pt}\end{center}

\hypertarget{whites-neural-network-test}{%
\subsection{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{➤ White's Neural Network
Test}}{➤ White's Neural Network Test}}\label{whites-neural-network-test}}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  \textbf{Neural Network MSE on residuals:} \textbf{11224.51}\\
  📌 \textbf{Interpretation:}\\
\item
  Residuals are better explained by a \textbf{linear model}.\\
\item
  No strong evidence that nonlinearity in residuals significantly
  affects predictions.
\end{itemize}

    \textbf{ARIMA , ARNN \& ARIMA-ARNN}

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{29}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{k+kn}{import}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{numpy}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k}{as}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{np}
\PY{k+kn}{import}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{pandas}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k}{as}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{pd}
\PY{k+kn}{import}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{matplotlib}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{pyplot}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k}{as}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{plt}
\PY{k+kn}{from}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{statsmodels}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{tsa}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{arima}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{model}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{ARIMA}
\PY{k+kn}{from}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{sklearn}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{neural\PYZus{}network}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{MLPRegressor}
\PY{k+kn}{from}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{sklearn}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{metrics}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}squared\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}absolute\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{r2\PYZus{}score}
\PY{k+kn}{from}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{sklearn}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{preprocessing}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{MinMaxScaler}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Load the data}
\PY{n}{data} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{pd}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{read\PYZus{}excel}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{AQI.xlsx}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Assuming \PYZsq{}AQI Index\PYZsq{} is the target variable}
\PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Date}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{pd}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{to\PYZus{}datetime}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Date}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{data}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{set\PYZus{}index}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Date}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{inplace}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{ts} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{AQI Index}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Split the data into training and testing sets}
\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}size} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{ts}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.8}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{ts}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{:}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}size}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{ts}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}size}\PY{p}{:}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{n}{train} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{train}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{asfreq}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{D}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{test} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{test}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{asfreq}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{D}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}


\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ARIMA Model}
\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{arima\PYZus{}model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{model} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{ARIMA}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{order}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{model\PYZus{}fit} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{fit}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{predictions} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{model\PYZus{}fit}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{forecast}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{steps}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{test}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{predictions}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ARNN Model}
\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{arnn\PYZus{}model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{scaler} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{MinMaxScaler}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}scaled} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{scaler}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{fit\PYZus{}transform}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{values}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reshape}\PY{p}{(}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}scaled} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{scaler}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{transform}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{test}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{values}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reshape}\PY{p}{(}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Prepare data for ARNN}
    \PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{create\PYZus{}dataset}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{look\PYZus{}back}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{X}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
        \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{i} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{range}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{look\PYZus{}back}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{X}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{:}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{i}\PY{o}{+}\PY{n}{look\PYZus{}back}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
            \PY{n}{Y}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{look\PYZus{}back}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{array}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{array}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{Y}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{n}{look\PYZus{}back} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}
    \PY{n}{trainX}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{trainY} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{create\PYZus{}dataset}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}scaled}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{look\PYZus{}back}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{testX}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{testY} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{create\PYZus{}dataset}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}scaled}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{look\PYZus{}back}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{n}{model} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{MLPRegressor}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{hidden\PYZus{}layer\PYZus{}sizes}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{10}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{10}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{max\PYZus{}iter}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1000}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{random\PYZus{}state}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{42}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{fit}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{trainX}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{trainY}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{n}{predictions} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{predict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{testX}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{predictions} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{scaler}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{inverse\PYZus{}transform}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{predictions}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reshape}\PY{p}{(}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Adjust test size to match predictions}
    \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}adjusted} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{test}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{iloc}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{look\PYZus{}back}\PY{p}{:}\PY{p}{]}

    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}adjusted}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{predictions}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{flatten}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ARIMA\PYZhy{}ARNN Hybrid Model}
\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{arima\PYZus{}arnn\PYZus{}hybrid}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{arima\PYZus{}predictions} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{arima\PYZus{}model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}adjusted}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{arnn\PYZus{}predictions} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{arnn\PYZus{}model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Combine predictions (simple average)}
    \PY{n}{hybrid\PYZus{}predictions} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{arima\PYZus{}predictions}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{:}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{arnn\PYZus{}predictions}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{arnn\PYZus{}predictions}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}adjusted}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{hybrid\PYZus{}predictions}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Evaluate models}
\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{evaluate\PYZus{}model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{predictions}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}features}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{mse} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}squared\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{predictions}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{rmse} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sqrt}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{mse}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{mae} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}absolute\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{predictions}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{mape} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{abs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{test} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{predictions}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{test}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mi}{100}
    \PY{n}{r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{r2\PYZus{}score}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{predictions}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Adjusted R² Calculation}
    \PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{test}\PY{p}{)}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Number of samples}
    \PY{n}{adj\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{r2}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}features} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{rmse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mae}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mape}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{r2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{adj\PYZus{}r2}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Fit and evaluate ARIMA}
\PY{n}{arima\PYZus{}predictions} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{arima\PYZus{}model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{arima\PYZus{}rmse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{arima\PYZus{}mae}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{arima\PYZus{}mape}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{arima\PYZus{}r2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{arima\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{evaluate\PYZus{}model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{arima\PYZus{}predictions}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Fit and evaluate ARNN}
\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}adjusted}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{arnn\PYZus{}predictions} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{arnn\PYZus{}model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{arnn\PYZus{}rmse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{arnn\PYZus{}mae}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{arnn\PYZus{}mape}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{arnn\PYZus{}r2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{arnn\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{evaluate\PYZus{}model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}adjusted}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{arnn\PYZus{}predictions}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Fit and evaluate ARIMA\PYZhy{}ARNN Hybrid}
\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}adjusted}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{hybrid\PYZus{}predictions} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{arima\PYZus{}arnn\PYZus{}hybrid}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{hybrid\PYZus{}rmse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{hybrid\PYZus{}mae}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{hybrid\PYZus{}mape}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{hybrid\PYZus{}r2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{hybrid\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{evaluate\PYZus{}model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}adjusted}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{hybrid\PYZus{}predictions}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Function to print evaluation results neatly}
\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{print\PYZus{}evaluation\PYZus{}results}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{model\PYZus{}name}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{rmse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mae}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mape}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{r2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{adj\PYZus{}r2}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{o}{*}\PY{l+m+mi}{60}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{model\PYZus{}name}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ Model Evaluation Metrics}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{o}{*}\PY{l+m+mi}{60}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Metric}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZlt{}20}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Value}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{o}{*}\PY{l+m+mi}{60}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{RMSE}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZlt{}20}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{rmse}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{MAE}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZlt{}20}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{mae}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{MAPE (}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{)}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZlt{}20}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{mape}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{R²}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZlt{}20}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{r2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.4f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Adjusted R²}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZlt{}20}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{adj\PYZus{}r2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.4f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{o}{*}\PY{l+m+mi}{60}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Print evaluation results for each model}
\PY{n}{print\PYZus{}evaluation\PYZus{}results}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ARIMA}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{arima\PYZus{}rmse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{arima\PYZus{}mae}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{arima\PYZus{}mape}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{arima\PYZus{}r2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{arima\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{print\PYZus{}evaluation\PYZus{}results}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ARNN}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{arnn\PYZus{}rmse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{arnn\PYZus{}mae}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{arnn\PYZus{}mape}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{arnn\PYZus{}r2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{arnn\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2}\PY{p}{)}

    \hypertarget{interpretations}{%
\section{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{Interpretations}}{Interpretations}}\label{interpretations}}

\hypertarget{arima-model-performance}{%
\subsection{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{➤ ARIMA Model
Performance}}{➤ ARIMA Model Performance}}\label{arima-model-performance}}

\begin{quote}
\textbf{🔹 Key Observations:} - \textbf{High RMSE (123.83) \& MAE
(109.88)} → Large errors in predictions. - \textbf{Very high MAPE
(92.93\%)} → On average, predictions deviate by \textasciitilde93\% from
actual values. - \textbf{Negative R² (-0.4911)} → The model performs
worse than simply predicting the mean of the data. - \textbf{Adjusted R²
(-0.4939)} confirms poor performance.
\end{quote}

📌 \textbf{Conclusion:}\\
\hspace*{0.333em}\hspace*{0.333em}\hspace*{0.333em}\hspace*{0.333em}ARIMA
alone does not capture AQI trends effectively.\\
\hspace*{0.333em}\hspace*{0.333em}\hspace*{0.333em}\hspace*{0.333em}It
struggles to predict variations in AQI, possibly due to nonlinear
patterns in the data.

\begin{center}\rule{0.5\linewidth}{0.5pt}\end{center}

\hypertarget{arnn-artificial-neural-network-model-performance}{%
\subsection{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{➤ ARNN (Artificial Neural Network)
Model
Performance}}{➤ ARNN (Artificial Neural Network) Model Performance}}\label{arnn-artificial-neural-network-model-performance}}

\begin{quote}
\textbf{🔹 Key Observations:} - \textbf{Lower RMSE (41.48) \& MAE
(30.54)} → Significantly reduced errors compared to ARIMA. -
\textbf{Lower MAPE (19.91\%)} → Predictions are much closer to actual
values. - \textbf{High R² (0.8330)} → The model explains \textbf{83.3\%}
of the variance in the data. - \textbf{Adjusted R² (0.8326)} → Minimal
overfitting.
\end{quote}

📌 \textbf{Conclusion:}\\
\hspace*{0.333em}\hspace*{0.333em}\hspace*{0.333em}\hspace*{0.333em}ARNN
performs significantly better than ARIMA.\\
\hspace*{0.333em}\hspace*{0.333em}\hspace*{0.333em}\hspace*{0.333em}It
captures nonlinear dependencies better, leading to improved
predictions.\\
\hspace*{0.333em}\hspace*{0.333em}\hspace*{0.333em}\hspace*{0.333em}However,
ARNN models require careful tuning (\textbf{e.g., number of neurons,
epochs}) to avoid overfitting.

\begin{center}\rule{0.5\linewidth}{0.5pt}\end{center}

\hypertarget{arima-arnn-hybrid-model-performance}{%
\subsection{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{➤ ARIMA-ARNN Hybrid Model
Performance}}{➤ ARIMA-ARNN Hybrid Model Performance}}\label{arima-arnn-hybrid-model-performance}}

\begin{quote}
\textbf{🔹 Key Observations:} - \textbf{Moderate RMSE (74.05) \& MAE
(64.60)} → Errors are reduced compared to ARIMA but higher than ARNN. -
\textbf{MAPE (51.29\%)} → Improvement over ARIMA but worse than ARNN. -
\textbf{Moderate R² (0.4676)} → Explains \textbf{46.76\%} of the
variance (\textbf{better than ARIMA but weaker than ARNN}). -
\textbf{Adjusted R² (0.4665)} supports this conclusion.
\end{quote}

📌 \textbf{Conclusion:}\\
\hspace*{0.333em}\hspace*{0.333em}\hspace*{0.333em}\hspace*{0.333em}The
hybrid model improves ARIMA but underperforms compared to ARNN alone.\\
\hspace*{0.333em}\hspace*{0.333em}\hspace*{0.333em}\hspace*{0.333em}ARIMA
contributes to linear patterns, while ARNN captures nonlinearities.\\
\hspace*{0.333em}\hspace*{0.333em}\hspace*{0.333em}\hspace*{0.333em}The
combination provides a middle-ground solution but still doesn't
outperform a pure ARNN.

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Function to create input\PYZhy{}output sequences}
\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{create\PYZus{}sequences}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{look\PYZus{}back}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{X}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{i} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{range}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{look\PYZus{}back}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{X}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{:}\PY{n}{i} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{look\PYZus{}back}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{Y}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{look\PYZus{}back}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{array}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{array}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{Y}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n}{look\PYZus{}back} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{5}
\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}train} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{create\PYZus{}sequences}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{AQI Index}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{values}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{look\PYZus{}back}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Reshape for LSTM, GRU, and TCN (samples, timesteps, features)}
\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reshape}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reshape}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Function to train models and evaluate performance}
\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{train\PYZus{}model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{model}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{model\PYZus{}name}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{compile}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{optimizer}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{Adam}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{learning\PYZus{}rate}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mf}{0.001}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{loss}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{mse}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{fit}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{epochs}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{20}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{batch\PYZus{}size}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{16}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{verbose}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{validation\PYZus{}data}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{n}{predictions} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{predict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{predictions} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{scaler}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{inverse\PYZus{}transform}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{predictions}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reshape}\PY{p}{(}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{flatten}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}actual} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{scaler}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{inverse\PYZus{}transform}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}test}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reshape}\PY{p}{(}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{flatten}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Calculate evaluation metrics}
    \PY{n}{rmse} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sqrt}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}squared\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}actual}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{predictions}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{mae} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}absolute\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}actual}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{predictions}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{mape} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}absolute\PYZus{}percentage\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}actual}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{predictions}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{r2\PYZus{}score}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}actual}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{predictions}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}actual}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Tree\PYZhy{}based Models}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Flatten sequences for tree\PYZhy{}based models}
\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{prepare\PYZus{}tree\PYZus{}data}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}flattened} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{X}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reshape}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Flatten sequences (timesteps * features)}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}flattened}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y}

\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}tree}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}tree} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{prepare\PYZus{}tree\PYZus{}data}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}tree}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}tree} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{prepare\PYZus{}tree\PYZus{}data}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Function to train tree\PYZhy{}based models with plots}
\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{train\PYZus{}tree\PYZus{}model\PYZus{}with\PYZus{}plots}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{model}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{model\PYZus{}name}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{fit}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Generate predictions}
    \PY{n}{predictions} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{predict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{predictions} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{scaler}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{inverse\PYZus{}transform}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{predictions}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reshape}\PY{p}{(}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{flatten}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}actual} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{scaler}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{inverse\PYZus{}transform}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}test}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reshape}\PY{p}{(}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{flatten}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Calculate evaluation metrics}
    \PY{n}{rmse} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sqrt}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}squared\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}actual}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{predictions}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{mae} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}absolute\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}actual}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{predictions}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{mape} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}absolute\PYZus{}percentage\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}actual}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{predictions}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{r2\PYZus{}score}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}actual}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{predictions}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{Y\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}actual}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{p} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{n}{adj\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{r2}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{p} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Print evaluation metrics}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{model\PYZus{}name}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{ Model Evaluation Metrics}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}} \PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mi}{50}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Metric}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ }\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{o}{*}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{l+m+mi}{15}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Value}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}

    \hypertarget{key-observations-from-correlation-matrix}{%
\subsubsection{Key Observations from Correlation
Matrix}\label{key-observations-from-correlation-matrix}}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  \textbf{High Positive Correlations with AQI Index}:

  \begin{itemize}
  \tightlist
  \item
    PM2.5 (\textbf{0.90}), NO2 (\textbf{0.56}), NO (\textbf{0.52}), NOx
    (\textbf{0.54}), and CO (\textbf{0.37}) show relatively strong
    positive correlations with AQI.
  \item
    This suggests that these pollutants significantly contribute to
    deteriorating air quality.
  \end{itemize}
\item
  \textbf{Negative or Weak Correlations with AQI Index}:

  \begin{itemize}
  \tightlist
  \item
    Wind Speed (\textbf{-0.36}), Wind Direction (\textbf{-0.26}), and
    Relative Humidity (\textbf{-0.14}) show weak or negative
    correlations.
  \item
    This implies that stronger winds and higher humidity might help in
    dispersing pollutants, improving air quality.
  \end{itemize}
\item
  \textbf{Other Observations}:

  \begin{itemize}
  \tightlist
  \item
    Eth-Benzene, MP-Xylene, and Toluene have lower correlations with
    AQI, indicating they might not be the primary contributors to air
    pollution in this dataset.
  \end{itemize}
\end{itemize}

\hypertarget{conclusion}{%
\subsubsection{Conclusion:}\label{conclusion}}

🔹 \textbf{PM2.5, NO2, NO, NOx, and CO are key contributors to AQI
levels}, while wind and humidity seem to have a moderating effect on air
quality.

    \hypertarget{adf-test-results---my-interpretation}{%
\section{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{ADF Test Results - My
Interpretation}}{ADF Test Results - My Interpretation}}\label{adf-test-results---my-interpretation}}

\hypertarget{key-observations}{%
\subsection{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{Key
Observations:}}{Key Observations:}}\label{key-observations}}

\hypertarget{date-column}{%
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{1. Date
Column:}}{1. Date Column:}}\label{date-column}}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  The \textbf{p-value is 1.0}, which means the date column is
  \textbf{not stationary} (as expected).\\
\item
  Since it's just a time index, I don't need to apply differencing to
  it.
\end{itemize}

\hypertarget{aqi-index}{%
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{2. AQI
Index:}}{2. AQI Index:}}\label{aqi-index}}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  The \textbf{p-value is 0.001}, which is \textbf{less than 0.05},
  indicating that AQI is already \textbf{stationary}.\\
\item
  No differencing is required for this variable.
\end{itemize}

\hypertarget{other-variables}{%
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{3. Other
Variables:}}{3. Other Variables:}}\label{other-variables}}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  \textbf{PM2.5, NO, NO2, NOx, SO2, CO, Ozone, Benzene, and others all
  have very small p-values (\textless\textless{} 0.05),} meaning they
  are already \textbf{stationary}.\\
\item
  Since these variables don't need differencing, I can use them directly
  for modeling.
\end{itemize}

\hypertarget{conclusion}{%
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{4.
Conclusion:}}{4. Conclusion:}}\label{conclusion}}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  The \textbf{only non-stationary column is ``Date''}, but that doesn't
  affect my analysis.\\
\item
  Since almost all my variables are already stationary, I \textbf{don't
  need to apply differencing} before
  ba.seasonal\_decompose\texttt{.\ \ \ sa.seasonal\_decompose}).
\end{itemize}

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{35}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Load your dataset (assuming it\PYZsq{}s already preprocessed)}

\PY{n}{max\PYZus{}lag} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{5}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Define the maximum number of lags to test}

    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{Granger Causality Test: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{predictor}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ → }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{target\PYZus{}variable}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{try}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}result} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{grangercausalitytests}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{target\PYZus{}variable}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{predictor}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{max\PYZus{}lag}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Extract and print p\PYZhy{}values}

            \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Lag }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{lag}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{: p\PYZhy{}value = }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{p\PYZus{}value}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.5f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{k}{except} \PY{n+ne}{Exception} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n}{e}\PY{p}{:}

    \hypertarget{observations-from-granger-causality-test}{%
\subsection{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{Observations from Granger Causality
Test}}{Observations from Granger Causality Test}}\label{observations-from-granger-causality-test}}

Based on the Granger Causality test results, the following key
observations were made:

\hypertarget{strongly-significant-predictors-p-value-0.05-across-all-lags}{%
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{1️⃣ Strongly Significant
Predictors (p-value \textless{} 0.05 across all
lags)}}{1️⃣ Strongly Significant Predictors (p-value \textless{} 0.05 across all lags)}}\label{strongly-significant-predictors-p-value-0.05-across-all-lags}}

These variables consistently show a strong causal relationship with AQI
Index: - \textbf{PM2.5 (µg/m³)} - \textbf{NO (µg/m³)} - \textbf{NO2
(µg/m³)} - \textbf{NOx (ppb)} - \textbf{CO (mg/m³)} - \textbf{Benzene
(µg/m³)} - \textbf{Toluene (µg/m³)} - \textbf{Wind Speed (m/s)} -
\textbf{Wind Direction (deg)}

\hypertarget{partially-significant-predictors-p-value-0.05-in-some-lags-but-not-all}{%
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{2️⃣ Partially Significant
Predictors (p-value \textless{} 0.05 in some lags, but not
all)}}{2️⃣ Partially Significant Predictors (p-value \textless{} 0.05 in some lags, but not all)}}\label{partially-significant-predictors-p-value-0.05-in-some-lags-but-not-all}}

These variables may have a weaker or lag-dependent causal relationship
with AQI Index: - \textbf{SO2 (µg/m³)} → Significant at lags 2, 3, 4,
and 5 but not at lag 1. - \textbf{Eth-Benzene (µg/m³)} → Significant in
most lags except lag 1. - \textbf{MP-Xylene (µg/m³)} - \textbf{Relative
Humidity (\%)} → Significant in lags 2, 3, 4, and 5 but not at lag 1. -
\textbf{Solar Radiation (W/mt²)} → Significant in lags 3, 4, and 5 but
not in earlier lags.

\hypertarget{non-significant-predictors-p-value-0.05-in-all-lags}{%
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{3️⃣ Non-Significant Predictors
(p-value \textgreater{} 0.05 in all
lags)}}{3️⃣ Non-Significant Predictors (p-value \textgreater{} 0.05 in all lags)}}\label{non-significant-predictors-p-value-0.05-in-all-lags}}

These variables do not show strong evidence of causality with AQI Index:
- \textbf{Ozone (µg/m³)} - \textbf{Vertical Wind Speed (m/s)}

\hypertarget{conclusion}{%
\subsection{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{Conclusion}}{Conclusion}}\label{conclusion}}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  Pollutants like \textbf{PM2.5, NOx, CO, and Benzene} are
  \textbf{highly influential} in determining AQI Index.
\item
  \textbf{Wind Speed and Wind Direction} also strongly contribute to AQI
  fluctuations.
\item
  \textbf{Ozone and Vertical Wind Speed} do not have a statistically
  significant causal impact on AQI. ute to its prediction.
\end{itemize}

    \hypertarget{observations-from-the-box-plot}{%
\section{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{Observations from the Box
Plot}}{Observations from the Box Plot}}\label{observations-from-the-box-plot}}

\hypertarget{aqi-index}{%
\subsection{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{1. AQI
Index}}{1. AQI Index}}\label{aqi-index}}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  Has a wide range of values, showing high variability.
\item
  The median AQI is significantly high.
\item
  Several outliers are present at the upper end, indicating extreme
  pollution levels on certain days.
\end{itemize}

\hypertarget{pm2.5-uxb5gmuxb3}{%
\subsection{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{2. PM2.5
(µg/m³)}}{2. PM2.5 (µg/m³)}}\label{pm2.5-uxb5gmuxb3}}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  Shows a moderately large spread.
\item
  A significant number of outliers at the higher end, suggesting
  occasional spikes in PM2.5 concentration.
\item
  The median is lower than that of AQI but still relatively high.
\end{itemize}

\hypertarget{no-uxb5gmuxb3-no2-uxb5gmuxb3}{%
\subsection{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{3. NO (µg/m³) \& NO2
(µg/m³)}}{3. NO (µg/m³) \& NO2 (µg/m³)}}\label{no-uxb5gmuxb3-no2-uxb5gmuxb3}}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  These pollutants have much lower median values compared to AQI and
  PM2.5.
\item
  The spread is relatively small, but they have many outliers,
  suggesting that while most values remain low, occasional peaks occur.
\end{itemize}

\hypertarget{conclusion}{%
\subsection{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{Conclusion}}{Conclusion}}\label{conclusion}}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  AQI and PM2.5 are \textbf{highly variable}, with frequent high values
  and outliers.
\item
  NO and NO2 levels are generally lower but exhibit sporadic extreme
  values.
\item
  The presence of numerous outliers, especially in PM2.5, suggests
  \textbf{periodic pollution spikes}, likely due to specific external
  events like weather conditions, traffic congestion, or industrial
  emissions. inter months?).
\end{itemize}

    \hypertarget{handle-outliers-using-winsorization---capping}{%
\subsubsection{Handle Outliers (Using Winsorization -
Capping)}\label{handle-outliers-using-winsorization---capping}}

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{41}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{k+kn}{import}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{numpy}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k}{as}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{np}
\PY{k+kn}{import}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{pandas}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k}{as}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{pd}
\PY{k+kn}{from}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{scipy}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{stats}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{mstats}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{winsorize}
\PY{k+kn}{import}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{seaborn}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k}{as}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{sns}
\PY{k+kn}{import}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{matplotlib}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{pyplot}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k}{as}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{plt}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Function to apply Winsorization with 10\PYZpc{}\PYZhy{}90\PYZpc{} threshold}
\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{winsorize\PYZus{}column}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{column}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{lower}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mf}{0.10}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{upper}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mf}{0.90}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{column}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{winsorize}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{column}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{limits}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{lower}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{n}{upper}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{df}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Copy original dataset}
\PY{n}{AQI\PYZus{}Pred\PYZus{}winsorized} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{AQI\PYZus{}Pred}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{copy}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Apply Winsorization to each numerical column}
\PY{n}{columns} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{AQI Index}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{PM2.5 (µg/m³)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{NO (µg/m³)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{NO2 (µg/m³)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}
\PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{col} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{columns}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{AQI\PYZus{}Pred\PYZus{}winsorized} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{winsorize\PYZus{}column}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{AQI\PYZus{}Pred\PYZus{}winsorized}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{col}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Plot boxplot after Winsorization}
\PY{n}{plt}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{figure}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{figsize}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{10}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{sns}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{boxplot}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{data}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{AQI\PYZus{}Pred\PYZus{}winsorized}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{plt}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{title}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{After Winsorization (10}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZpc{} \PYZhy{} 90\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{plt}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{show}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    \begin{center}
    \adjustimage{max size={0.9\linewidth}{0.9\paperheight}}{output_49_0.png}
    \end{center}
    { \hspace*{\fill} \\}
    
    \hypertarget{observation-winsorization-10---90}{%
\section{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{Observation: Winsorization (10\% -
90\%)}}{Observation: Winsorization (10\% - 90\%)}}\label{observation-winsorization-10---90}}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  \textbf{Outliers have been significantly reduced}, as extreme values
  are now capped at the 10th and 90th percentiles.
\item
  \textbf{AQI Index and PM2.5 values are now more concentrated}, showing
  better stability in the data distribution.
\item
  \textbf{NO and NO₂ have minimal outliers}, indicating that
  Winsorization has successfully handled extreme values.
\item
  \textbf{Compared to previous Winsorization thresholds (e.g.,
  5\%-95\%), the whiskers are shorter}, meaning more extreme values have
  been adjusted.
\item
  \textbf{Data retains its distribution shape} while removing excessive
  fluctuations.
\end{itemize}

This Winsorization approach effectively smooths out extreme values while
keeping essential variations for model fitting.

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{42}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Plot AQI Index over time}
\PY{n}{plt}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{figure}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{figsize}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{12}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{6}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

    \hypertarget{observations-from-time-series-plots}{%
\subsection{Observations from Time Series
Plots}\label{observations-from-time-series-plots}}

\hypertarget{aqi-index-over-time-top-plot}{%
\subsubsection{1. AQI Index Over Time (Top
Plot)}\label{aqi-index-over-time-top-plot}}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  The AQI Index goes up and down regularly, showing a repeating pattern.
\item
  There are many sharp increases, which means air pollution gets very
  high at times.
\item
  The values change a lot over time, showing that air quality is not
  stable.
\end{itemize}

\hypertarget{independent-variables-over-time-bottom-plot}{%
\subsubsection{2. Independent Variables Over Time (Bottom
Plot)}\label{independent-variables-over-time-bottom-plot}}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  PM2.5 (Green) has the highest peaks, which suggests it affects AQI the
  most.
\item
  NO (Orange) and NO₂ (Red) stay lower but still rise at certain times.
\item
  All three variables follow a pattern over time, which may be linked to
  seasons.
\end{itemize}

\hypertarget{next-steps}{%
\subsubsection{3. Next Steps}\label{next-steps}}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  Check if AQI is closely related to PM2.5, NO, and NO₂.
\item
  Break down the time series into trends and seasonal effects.
\item
  Use moving averages to smooth out the ups and downs and see patterns
  clearly.
\end{itemize}

    \hypertarget{observations-from-time-series-decomposition}{%
\subsubsection{Observations from Time Series
Decomposition}\label{observations-from-time-series-decomposition}}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  \textbf{Trend}: The AQI Index shows long-term patterns, with periods
  of increase and decrease over time.\\
\item
  \textbf{Seasonal Component}: There are repeating patterns at regular
  intervals, indicating seasonal effects on AQI.\\
\item
  \textbf{Residual Component}: The remaining variations are random,
  capturing unexpected changes or external factors.\\
\item
  The combination of trend and seasonality suggests that AQI is
  influenced by both long-term changes and repeating seasonal patterns.
\end{itemize}

    \hypertarget{default-lag-selection-rule}{%
\subsection{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{Default Lag Selection
Rule}}{Default Lag Selection Rule}}\label{default-lag-selection-rule}}

If your dataset has \textbf{N observations}, a common heuristic is:\\
- \textbf{max lags = N/4}

\hypertarget{example-calculations}{%
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{Example
Calculations}}{Example Calculations}}\label{example-calculations}}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  If you have \textbf{365 daily AQI values}, use:
\item
  \textbf{max lags =365/4 = approx 90}
\item
  If you have \textbf{1000 observations}, use:
\item
  \textbf{max lags = 1000/4 = 250}
\end{itemize}

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{45}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{n}{N} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{AQI\PYZus{}Pred\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Number of observations}
\PY{n}{max\PYZus{}lags} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{N} \PY{o}{/}\PY{o}{/} \PY{l+m+mi}{4}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Integer division}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Suggested max lags: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{max\PYZus{}lags}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
Suggested max lags: 649
    \end{Verbatim}

    \hypertarget{why-is-50-a-good-choice}{%
\subsubsection{✅ Why is 50 a Good
Choice?}\label{why-is-50-a-good-choice}}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  \textbf{More practical}: Large lags (like 649) can cause overfitting
  and slow computation.\\
\item
  \textbf{Efficient}: Usually, useful information is captured within the
  first \textbf{50-100 lags} in time series.\\
\item
  \textbf{ACF/PACF plots}: If significant spikes appear within
  \textbf{50 lags}, it's enough for model selection.
\end{itemize}
