    \hypertarget{interpretation-of-seasonal-decomposition}{%
\subsection{Interpretation of Seasonal
Decomposition}\label{interpretation-of-seasonal-decomposition}}

\hypertarget{observed-original-aqi-index}{%
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{1. \textbf{Observed (Original AQI
Index)}}{1. Observed (Original AQI Index)}}\label{observed-original-aqi-index}}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  The first plot represents the original AQI Index time series.
\item
  Noticeable fluctuations and repeating patterns suggest a strong
  seasonal component.
\end{itemize}

\hypertarget{trend-component}{%
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{2. \textbf{Trend
Component}}{2. Trend Component}}\label{trend-component}}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  The AQI Index shows a \textbf{downward trend from 2018 to 2021},
  followed by a slight increase and then a decline.
\item
  This indicates long-term variations in air quality levels over time.
\end{itemize}

\hypertarget{seasonal-component}{%
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{3. \textbf{Seasonal
Component}}{3. Seasonal Component}}\label{seasonal-component}}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  A clear \textbf{seasonal pattern} is observed, likely driven by annual
  cycles in environmental or human activities.
\item
  The peaks and troughs repeat consistently, confirming seasonality.
\end{itemize}

\hypertarget{residuals-noise}{%
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{4. \textbf{Residuals
(Noise)}}{4. Residuals (Noise)}}\label{residuals-noise}}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  The residuals appear randomly distributed, meaning the model
  successfully extracted trend and seasonality.
\item
  Some fluctuations suggest the presence of anomalies or unexpected
  external influences.
\end{itemize}

\hypertarget{implications-for-sarimax-modeling}{%
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{Implications for SARIMAX
Modeling}}{Implications for SARIMAX Modeling}}\label{implications-for-sarimax-modeling}}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  The presence of \textbf{seasonality} suggests that a \textbf{seasonal
  order (P, D, Q, s)} should be included.
\item
  Since the \textbf{ADF test confirmed stationarity}, we set \textbf{D =
  0}.
\item
  The \textbf{trend variations} indicate that incorporating
  \textbf{exogenous variables (PM2.5, NO, NO2)} might improve the model.
\end{itemize}

    \hypertarget{fitting-sarimax-model}{%
\subsubsection{Fitting SARIMAX Model}\label{fitting-sarimax-model}}

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{47}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{k+kn}{import}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{pandas}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k}{as}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{pd}
\PY{k+kn}{import}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{statsmodels}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{api}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k}{as}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{sm}
\PY{k+kn}{import}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{matplotlib}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{pyplot}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k}{as}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{plt}
\PY{k+kn}{import}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{numpy}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k}{as}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{np}
\PY{k+kn}{from}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{sklearn}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{metrics}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}absolute\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}squared\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{r2\PYZus{}score}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Load dataset}
\PY{n}{df} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{AQI\PYZus{}Pred\PYZus{}winsorized}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{copy}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{index} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{pd}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{to\PYZus{}datetime}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{df} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{asfreq}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{D}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Drop missing values}
\PY{n}{df} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{dropna}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{subset}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{AQI Index}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{PM2.5 (µg/m³)}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{NO (µg/m³)}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{NO2 (µg/m³)}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Define target and regressors}
\PY{n}{endog} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{AQI Index}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}
\PY{n}{exog} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{PM2.5 (µg/m³)}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{NO (µg/m³)}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{NO2 (µg/m³)}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} =========================}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Train\PYZhy{}Test Split}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} =========================}
\PY{n}{split} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.8}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{endog\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{endog\PYZus{}test} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{endog}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{iloc}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{:}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{endog}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{iloc}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{:}\PY{p}{]}
\PY{n}{exog\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{exog\PYZus{}test}   \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{exog}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{iloc}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{:}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{exog}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{iloc}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{:}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} =========================}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Generalized SARIMAX Model (reduced overfitting)}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} =========================}
\PY{n}{model} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{sm}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{tsa}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{SARIMAX}\PY{p}{(}
    \PY{n}{endog\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{exog}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{exog\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{order}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}             \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} simpler AR structure}
    \PY{n}{seasonal\PYZus{}order}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{7}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} WEEKLY seasonality (Delhi traffic + pollution cycle)}
    \PY{n}{enforce\PYZus{}stationarity}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{enforce\PYZus{}invertibility}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}
\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n}{results} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{fit}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{disp}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{False}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{results}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{summary}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} =========================}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Predictions}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} =========================}
\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}pred} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{results}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{predict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{start}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{endog\PYZus{}train}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{end}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{endog\PYZus{}train}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{exog}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{exog\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}pred}  \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{results}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{predict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{start}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{endog\PYZus{}test}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}  \PY{n}{end}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{endog\PYZus{}test}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}  \PY{n}{exog}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{exog\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} =========================}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Performance Evaluation}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} =========================}
\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{evaluate}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{true}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{pred}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{mae} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}absolute\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{true}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{pred}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{rmse} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sqrt}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}squared\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{true}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{pred}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{mape} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{abs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{true} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{pred}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{true}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mi}{100}
    \PY{n}{r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{r2\PYZus{}score}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{true}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{pred}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{mae}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{rmse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mape}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{r2}

\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mae}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}rmse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mape}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{evaluate}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{endog\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mae}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}rmse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mape}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}r2}     \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{evaluate}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{endog\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{,}  \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} =========================}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Full Metrics (Train \PYZam{} Test)}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} =========================}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Function to compute all metrics}
\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{full\PYZus{}metrics}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{true}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{pred}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{mae} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}absolute\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{true}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{pred}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{mse} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}squared\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{true}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{pred}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{rmse} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sqrt}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{mse}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{mape} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{abs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{true} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{pred}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{true}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mi}{100}
    \PY{n}{r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{r2\PYZus{}score}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{true}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{pred}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{true}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{p} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{exog}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} number of regressors}
    \PY{n}{adj\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{r2}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{p} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{mae}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{rmse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mape}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{r2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{adj\PYZus{}r2}

\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mae2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mse2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}rmse2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mape2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}r2\PYZus{}2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{full\PYZus{}metrics}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{endog\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mae2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mse2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}rmse2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mape2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}r2\PYZus{}2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{full\PYZus{}metrics}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{endog\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{================ FULL TRAIN METRICS ================}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mae2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MSE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mse2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{RMSE       : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}rmse2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAPE       : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mape2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{R²         : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}r2\PYZus{}2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Adj. R²    : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{================ FULL TEST METRICS =================}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mae2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MSE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mse2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{k+kn}{import}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{os}
\PY{k+kn}{import}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{random}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Set seeds for reproducibility}
\PY{n}{seed} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{42}
\PY{n}{os}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{environ}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{PYTHONHASHSEED}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{str}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{seed}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{random}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{seed}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{seed}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{k+kn}{import}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{numpy}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k}{as}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{np}
\PY{k+kn}{import}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{pandas}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k}{as}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{pd}
\PY{k+kn}{import}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{tensorflow}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k}{as}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{tf}
\PY{k+kn}{from}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{tensorflow}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{keras}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{models}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{Sequential}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Load dataset}

\PY{n}{df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{index} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{pd}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{to\PYZus{}datetime}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{)}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Convert index to datetime}
\PY{n}{df} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{asfreq}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{D}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Ensure daily frequency}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Drop rows with missing values}
\PY{n}{df} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{dropna}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{subset}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{PM2.5 (µg/m³)}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{NO (µg/m³)}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{NO2 (µg/m³)}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{AQI Index}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Selecting features and target variable}
\PY{n}{features} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{PM2.5 (µg/m³)}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{NO (µg/m³)}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{NO2 (µg/m³)}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}
\PY{n}{target} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{AQI Index}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Normalize data}
\PY{n}{scaler} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{MinMaxScaler}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{df\PYZus{}scaled} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{scaler}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{fit\PYZus{}transform}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{features} \PY{o}{+} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{target}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{df\PYZus{}scaled} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{pd}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{DataFrame}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{df\PYZus{}scaled}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{columns}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{features} \PY{o}{+} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{target}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{index}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Define sequences for LSTM}
\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{create\PYZus{}sequences}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{seq\PYZus{}length}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{X}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{i} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{range}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{data}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{seq\PYZus{}length}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{X}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{data}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{iloc}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{:}\PY{n}{i} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{seq\PYZus{}length}\PY{p}{,} \PY{p}{:}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{values}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{y}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{data}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{iloc}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{seq\PYZus{}length}\PY{p}{,} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{array}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{array}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Set sequence length}
\PY{n}{SEQ\PYZus{}LENGTH} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{30}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Split into training and testing sets}
\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}size} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{df\PYZus{}scaled}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.8}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}data}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}data} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{df\PYZus{}scaled}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{iloc}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{:}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}size}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{df\PYZus{}scaled}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{iloc}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}size}\PY{p}{:}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Prepare sequences}
\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}train} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{create\PYZus{}sequences}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}data}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{SEQ\PYZus{}LENGTH}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{create\PYZus{}sequences}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}data}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{SEQ\PYZus{}LENGTH}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Reshape for LSTM}

\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reshape}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{SEQ\PYZus{}LENGTH}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{features}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Build LSTM model with regularization and dropout}
\PY{n}{model} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Sequential}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{[}
    \PY{n}{LSTM}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{50}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{return\PYZus{}sequences}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{input\PYZus{}shape}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{SEQ\PYZus{}LENGTH}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{features}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{Dropout}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mf}{0.2}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{LSTM}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{50}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{return\PYZus{}sequences}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{False}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{Dropout}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mf}{0.2}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{25}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{kernel\PYZus{}regularizer}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{l2}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mf}{0.001}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Compile model}
\PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{compile}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{optimizer}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{adam}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{loss}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{mean\PYZus{}squared\PYZus{}error}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} EarlyStopping callback}

    \PY{n}{monitor}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{val\PYZus{}loss}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{patience}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{restore\PYZus{}best\PYZus{}weights}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}
\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Train model}

    \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,}

    \PY{n}{epochs}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{50}\PY{p}{,}

    \PY{n}{callbacks}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{early\PYZus{}stop}\PY{p}{]}
\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Rescale predictions}

    \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{hstack}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{zeros}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{features}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reshape}\PY{p}{(}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{:}\PY{p}{,} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}
\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}rescaled} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{scaler}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{inverse\PYZus{}transform}\PY{p}{(}
    \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{hstack}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{zeros}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{features}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reshape}\PY{p}{(}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{:}\PY{p}{,} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Compute TEST metrics}
\PY{n}{mae} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}absolute\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}rescaled}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred\PYZus{}rescaled}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{mse} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}squared\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}rescaled}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred\PYZus{}rescaled}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n}{adjusted\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{r2}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{p} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mae}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MSE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mse}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{RMSE       : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}rmse}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAPE       : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mape}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{R²         : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}r2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Adjusted R²: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{================ TEST METRICS (LSTM) =================}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{mae}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MSE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{mse}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{RMSE       : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{rmse}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAPE       : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{mape}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{R²         : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{r2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Adjusted R²: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{adjusted\PYZus{}r2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==============================}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} GENERALIZATION CHECK}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==============================}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{================ MODEL DIAGNOSIS =================}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{k}{if} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{r2} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.1}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o+ow}{and} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}rmse} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{n}{rmse} \PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.8}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{⚠️ LSTM is OVERFITTING (Train \PYZgt{}\PYZgt{} Test performance)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{k}{elif} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.3} \PY{o+ow}{and} \PY{n}{r2} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.3}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{⚠️ LSTM is UNDERFITTING (not learning patterns well)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{✅ LSTM is WELL\PYZhy{}GENERALIZED (Train ≈ Test performance)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Plot actual vs predicted values}
\PY{n}{plt}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{figure}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{figsize}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{10}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n}{plt}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{plot}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}size} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{SEQ\PYZus{}LENGTH}\PY{p}{:}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred\PYZus{}rescaled}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{label}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Predicted AQI (LSTM)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{color}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{red}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{linestyle}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{dashed}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\subsection{XGBOOST}\label{xgboost}}

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{49}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{k+kn}{import}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{pandas}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k}{as}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{pd}
\PY{k+kn}{import}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{numpy}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k}{as}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{np}
\PY{k+kn}{from}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{xgboost}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{XGBRegressor}
\PY{k+kn}{from}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{sklearn}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{model\PYZus{}selection}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}split}
\PY{k+kn}{from}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{sklearn}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{metrics}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}absolute\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}squared\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{r2\PYZus{}score}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Load dataset}
\PY{n}{df} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{AQI\PYZus{}Pred\PYZus{}winsorized}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{copy}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{index} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{pd}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{to\PYZus{}datetime}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{df} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{asfreq}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{D}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Features and target}
\PY{n}{X} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{PM2.5 (µg/m³)}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{NO (µg/m³)}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{NO2 (µg/m³)}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{]}
\PY{n}{y} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{AQI Index}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Train\PYZhy{}test split (80\PYZpc{} train, 20\PYZpc{} test)}
\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}split}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}size}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mf}{0.2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{shuffle}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{False}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} =============================}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}  Generalized XGBoost Model}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} =============================}
\PY{n}{xgb\PYZus{}model} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{XGBRegressor}\PY{p}{(}
    \PY{n}{objective}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{reg:squarederror}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}estimators}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{250}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{learning\PYZus{}rate}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mf}{0.04}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{max\PYZus{}depth}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{min\PYZus{}child\PYZus{}weight}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{subsample}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mf}{0.6}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{colsample\PYZus{}bytree}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mf}{0.6}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{reg\PYZus{}lambda}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mf}{2.0}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{reg\PYZus{}alpha}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mf}{1.0}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{random\PYZus{}state}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{42}
\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Train model}
\PY{n}{xgb\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{fit}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Predictions}
\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{xgb\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{predict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}pred} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{xgb\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{predict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} =============================}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}  Metrics Function}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} =============================}
\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{full\PYZus{}metrics}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}features}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{mae} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}absolute\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{mse} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}squared\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{rmse} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sqrt}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{mse}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{mape} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{abs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mi}{100}
    \PY{n}{r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{r2\PYZus{}score}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{adj\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{r2}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}features} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{mae}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{rmse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mape}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{r2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{adj\PYZus{}r2}

\PY{n}{p} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{X}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} number of features}

\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mae}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}rmse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mape}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}r2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{full\PYZus{}metrics}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{p}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mae}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}rmse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mape}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}r2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{full\PYZus{}metrics}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{p}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} =============================}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}  Print Metrics}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} =============================}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{================ TRAIN METRICS ================}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mae}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MSE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mse}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{RMSE       : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}rmse}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAPE       : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mape}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{R²         : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}r2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Adjusted R²: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{================ TEST METRICS =================}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mae}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MSE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mse}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{RMSE       : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}rmse}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAPE       : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mape}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{R²         : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}r2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Adjusted R²: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{====================================================}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Overfitting Check}
\PY{k}{if} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}rmse} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}rmse} \PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.8}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o+ow}{and} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{+} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ Model is OVERFITTING (Train \PYZgt{}\PYZgt{} Test)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{k}{elif} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.3} \PY{o+ow}{and} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.3}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ Model is UNDERFITTING (Model too simple)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ Model is WELL\PYZhy{}GENERALIZED (Train ≈ Test)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

\subsection{Prophet}\label{prophet}}

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{63}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{k+kn}{import}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{pandas}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k}{as}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{pd}
\PY{k+kn}{import}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{numpy}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k}{as}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{np}
\PY{k+kn}{from}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{prophet}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{Prophet}
\PY{k+kn}{from}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{sklearn}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{metrics}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}absolute\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}squared\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{r2\PYZus{}score}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Load dataset}
\PY{n}{df} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{AQI\PYZus{}Pred\PYZus{}winsorized}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{copy}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Replace with your actual dataset}
\PY{n}{df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reset\PYZus{}index}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{inplace}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{)}      \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Ensure datetime index becomes a column}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Rename columns for Prophet}
\PY{n}{df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{columns} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{ds}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{y}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{PM2.5}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{NO}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{NO2}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZsq{}ds\PYZsq{} = datetime, \PYZsq{}y\PYZsq{} = AQI Index}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Initialize Prophet model}
\PY{n}{prophet\PYZus{}model} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Prophet}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Add external regressors}
\PY{n}{prophet\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{add\PYZus{}regressor}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{PM2.5}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{prophet\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{add\PYZus{}regressor}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{NO}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{prophet\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{add\PYZus{}regressor}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{NO2}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Fit the model}
\PY{n}{prophet\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{fit}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{ds}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{y}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{PM2.5}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{NO}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{NO2}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Generate predictions on training data}
\PY{n}{forecast} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{prophet\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{predict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{ds}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{PM2.5}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{NO}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{NO2}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Extract actual and predicted values}
\PY{n}{actual} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{y}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}
\PY{n}{predicted} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{forecast}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{yhat}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Calculate error metrics}
\PY{n}{mae} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}absolute\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{actual}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{predicted}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{mse} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}squared\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{actual}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{predicted}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{rmse} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sqrt}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{mse}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{mape} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{abs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{actual} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{predicted}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{actual}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mi}{100}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Mean Absolute Percentage Error}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Calculate R² and Adjusted R²}
\PY{n}{r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{r2\PYZus{}score}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{actual}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{predicted}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{actual}\PY{p}{)}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Number of observations}
\PY{n}{p} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{3}            \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Number of predictors (PM2.5, NO, NO2)}
\PY{n}{adjusted\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{r2}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{p} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==============================}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ✅ Overfitting Check (Train vs Test) WITH FULL METRICS}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==============================}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Use last 20\PYZpc{} data for testing}
\PY{n}{split} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.8}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}df} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{iloc}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{:}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{]}
\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}df}  \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{iloc}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{:}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Train model again on train only (same settings)}
\PY{n}{prophet\PYZus{}model\PYZus{}test} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Prophet}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{prophet\PYZus{}model\PYZus{}test}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{add\PYZus{}regressor}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{PM2.5}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{prophet\PYZus{}model\PYZus{}test}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{add\PYZus{}regressor}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{NO}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{prophet\PYZus{}model\PYZus{}test}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{add\PYZus{}regressor}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{NO2}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{prophet\PYZus{}model\PYZus{}test}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{fit}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{ds}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{y}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{PM2.5}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{NO}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{NO2}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Predictions for train \PYZam{} test}
\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}forecast} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{prophet\PYZus{}model\PYZus{}test}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{predict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{ds}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{PM2.5}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{NO}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{NO2}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}forecast}  \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{prophet\PYZus{}model\PYZus{}test}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{predict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{ds}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{PM2.5}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{NO}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{NO2}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Function to compute full metrics}
\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{full\PYZus{}metrics}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{actual}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{predicted}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}features}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{mae} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}absolute\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{actual}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{predicted}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{mse} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}squared\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{actual}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{predicted}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{rmse} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sqrt}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{mse}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{mape} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{abs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{actual} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{predicted}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{actual}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mi}{100}
    \PY{n}{r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{r2\PYZus{}score}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{actual}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{predicted}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{actual}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{adj\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{r2}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}features} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{mae}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{rmse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mape}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{r2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{adj\PYZus{}r2}

\PY{n}{p} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{3}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} number of regressors}

\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mae}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}rmse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mape}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}r2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{full\PYZus{}metrics}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{y}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}forecast}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{yhat}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{p}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mae}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}rmse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mape}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}r2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{full\PYZus{}metrics}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{y}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}forecast}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{yhat}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{p}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Display Full Metrics}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{================ TRAIN METRICS ================}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mae}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MSE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mse}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{RMSE       : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}rmse}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAPE       : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mape}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{R²         : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}r2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Adjusted R²: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{================ TEST METRICS =================}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mae}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MSE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mse}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{RMSE       : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}rmse}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAPE       : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mape}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{R²         : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}r2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Adjusted R²: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{================================================}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Interpretation}
\PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}rmse} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}rmse} \PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mf}{1.3} \PY{o+ow}{and} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.1}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{⚠️ Model is OVERFITTING}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{k}{elif} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.3} \PY{o+ow}{and} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.3}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{⚠️ Model is UNDERFITTING}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{✅ Model is WELL\PYZhy{}GENERALIZED}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

    \textbf{RANDOM} \textbf{FOREST}

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{51}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{k+kn}{import}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{pandas}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k}{as}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{pd}
\PY{k+kn}{import}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{numpy}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k}{as}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{np}
\PY{k+kn}{from}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{sklearn}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{ensemble}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{RandomForestRegressor}
\PY{k+kn}{from}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{sklearn}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{model\PYZus{}selection}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}split}
\PY{k+kn}{from}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{sklearn}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{metrics}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}absolute\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}squared\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{r2\PYZus{}score}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Load dataset}
\PY{n}{df} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{AQI\PYZus{}Pred\PYZus{}winsorized}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{copy}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Replace AQI\PYZus{}Pred\PYZus{}model with your dataset}
\PY{n}{df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{index} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{pd}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{to\PYZus{}datetime}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{)}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Convert index to datetime}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Define features and target variable}
\PY{n}{features} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{PM2.5 (µg/m³)}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{NO (µg/m³)}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{NO2 (µg/m³)}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}
\PY{n}{target} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{AQI Index}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}

\PY{n}{X} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{features}\PY{p}{]}
\PY{n}{y} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{target}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Split data into training and testing sets}
\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}split}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}size}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mf}{0.2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{random\PYZus{}state}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{42}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Initialize Random Forest model}
\PY{n}{rf\PYZus{}model} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{RandomForestRegressor}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n\PYZus{}estimators}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{100}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{random\PYZus{}state}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{42}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Train the model}
\PY{n}{rf\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{fit}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Make predictions}
\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{rf\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{predict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Calculate evaluation metrics}
\PY{n}{mae} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}absolute\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{mse} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}squared\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{rmse} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sqrt}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{mse}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{r2\PYZus{}score}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Calculate Adjusted R²}
\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{)}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Sample size}
\PY{n}{p} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Number of predictors}
\PY{n}{adjusted\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{r2}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{p} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Calculate Mean Absolute Percentage Error (MAPE)}
\PY{n}{mape} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{abs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mi}{100}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==============================}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}  Overfitting Check (Train vs Test) with Full Metrics}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==============================}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Predictions on TRAIN data}
\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}pred} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{rf\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{predict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Function to compute all metrics}
\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{full\PYZus{}metrics}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}features}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{mae} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}absolute\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{mse} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}squared\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{rmse} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sqrt}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{mse}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{mape} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{abs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mi}{100}
    \PY{n}{r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{r2\PYZus{}score}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{adj\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{r2}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}features} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{mae}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{rmse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mape}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{r2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{adj\PYZus{}r2}

\PY{n}{p} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{X}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} number of input features}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Train metrics}
\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mae}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}rmse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mape}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}r2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{full\PYZus{}metrics}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{p}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Test metrics (already computed but reformat)}
\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mae}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}rmse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mape}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}r2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{full\PYZus{}metrics}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{p}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{================ TRAIN METRICS ================}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mae}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MSE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mse}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{RMSE       : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}rmse}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAPE       : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mape}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{R²         : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}r2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Adjusted R²: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{================ TEST METRICS =================}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mae}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MSE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mse}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{RMSE       : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}rmse}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAPE       : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mape}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{R²         : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}r2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Adjusted R²: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{================================================}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Interpretation}
\PY{k}{if} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.1}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o+ow}{and} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}rmse} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}rmse} \PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.8}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{⚠️ Model is OVERFITTING (train \PYZgt{}\PYZgt{} test performance)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{k}{elif} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.3} \PY{o+ow}{and} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.3}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{⚠️ Model is UNDERFITTING (model too simple / not learning patterns)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{✅ Model is WELL\PYZhy{}GENERALIZED (train ≈ test)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{k+kn}{import}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{pandas}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k}{as}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{pd}
\PY{k+kn}{import}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{numpy}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k}{as}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{np}
\PY{k+kn}{from}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{sklearn}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{ensemble}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{RandomForestRegressor}
\PY{k+kn}{from}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{sklearn}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{model\PYZus{}selection}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}split}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{GridSearchCV}
\PY{k+kn}{from}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{sklearn}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{metrics}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}absolute\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}squared\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{r2\PYZus{}score}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Load dataset}
\PY{n}{df} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{AQI\PYZus{}Pred\PYZus{}winsorized}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{copy}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Replace with your dataset}
\PY{n}{df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{index} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{pd}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{to\PYZus{}datetime}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{)}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Convert index to datetime}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Define features and target variable}
\PY{n}{features} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{PM2.5 (µg/m³)}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{NO (µg/m³)}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{NO2 (µg/m³)}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}
\PY{n}{target} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{AQI Index}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}

\PY{n}{X} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{features}\PY{p}{]}
\PY{n}{y} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{target}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Split data into training and testing sets}
\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}split}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}size}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mf}{0.2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{random\PYZus{}state}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{42}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Define hyperparameter grid}
\PY{n}{param\PYZus{}grid} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}
    \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{n\PYZus{}estimators}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{50}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{100}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{200}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Number of trees}
    \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{max\PYZus{}depth}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{10}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{15}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Maximum tree depth}
    \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{min\PYZus{}samples\PYZus{}split}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{10}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Minimum samples to split}
    \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{min\PYZus{}samples\PYZus{}leaf}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{4}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Minimum samples in a leaf}
    \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{max\PYZus{}features}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{sqrt}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{log2}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{k+kc}{None}\PY{p}{]}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Feature selection methods}
\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Initialize Random Forest model}
\PY{n}{rf\PYZus{}model} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{RandomForestRegressor}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{random\PYZus{}state}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{42}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Perform GridSearchCV for hyperparameter tuning}
\PY{n}{grid\PYZus{}search} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{GridSearchCV}\PY{p}{(}
    \PY{n}{estimator}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{rf\PYZus{}model}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{param\PYZus{}grid}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{param\PYZus{}grid}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{cv}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{scoring}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{r2}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{verbose}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}jobs}\PY{o}{=}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}
\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Fit GridSearch to training data}
\PY{n}{grid\PYZus{}search}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{fit}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Get the best parameters and model}
\PY{n}{best\PYZus{}params} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{grid\PYZus{}search}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{best\PYZus{}params\PYZus{}}
\PY{n}{best\PYZus{}model} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{grid\PYZus{}search}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{best\PYZus{}estimator\PYZus{}}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{Best Hyperparameters:}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{best\PYZus{}params}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Make predictions using the best model}
\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{best\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{predict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Define number of samples and features}
\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{)}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Number of test samples}
\PY{n}{p} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Number of features}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Evaluate model performance}
\PY{n}{mae} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}absolute\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{mse} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}squared\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{rmse} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sqrt}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{mse}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{r2\PYZus{}score}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{adjusted\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{r2}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{p} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Calculate Mean Absolute Percentage Error (MAPE)}
\PY{n}{mape} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{abs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mi}{100}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==============================}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ✅ Overfitting Check (Train vs Test) with Full Metrics}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==============================}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Predictions on TRAIN data using best model}
\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}pred} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{best\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{predict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Full Metrics Function}
\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{full\PYZus{}metrics}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}features}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{mae} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}absolute\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{mse} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}squared\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{rmse} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sqrt}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{mse}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{mape} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{abs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mi}{100}
    \PY{n}{r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{r2\PYZus{}score}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{adj\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{r2}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}features} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{mae}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{rmse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mape}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{r2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{adj\PYZus{}r2}

\PY{n}{p} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} number of features}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Compute Train Metrics}
\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mae}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}rmse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mape}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}r2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{full\PYZus{}metrics}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{p}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Compute Test Metrics (recomputed to match format)}
\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mae}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}rmse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mape}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}r2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{full\PYZus{}metrics}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{p}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{================ TRAIN METRICS ================}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mae}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MSE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mse}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{RMSE       : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}rmse}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAPE       : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mape}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{R²         : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}r2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.4f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Adjusted R²: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.4f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{================ TEST METRICS =================}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mae}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MSE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mse}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{RMSE       : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}rmse}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAPE       : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mape}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{R²         : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}r2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.4f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Adjusted R²: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.4f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{================================================}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Interpretation}
\PY{k}{if} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.1}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o+ow}{and} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}rmse} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}rmse} \PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.8}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{⚠️ Model is OVERFITTING (Train performance much better than Test)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{k}{elif} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.3} \PY{o+ow}{and} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.3}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{⚠️ Model is UNDERFITTING (Model too weak, not learning patterns)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{✅ Model is WELL\PYZhy{}GENERALIZED (Train and Test performance close)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}
