\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{k+kn}{from}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{sklearn}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{tree}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{DecisionTreeRegressor}
\PY{k+kn}{from}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{sklearn}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{metrics}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}absolute\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}squared\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{r2\PYZus{}score}
\PY{k+kn}{import}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{numpy}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{k}{as}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nn}{np}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ✅ Generalized (Pruned) Decision Tree Model}
\PY{n}{dt\PYZus{}model} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{DecisionTreeRegressor}\PY{p}{(}
    \PY{n}{max\PYZus{}depth}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{6}\PY{p}{,}            \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} limits tree depth → reduces overfitting}
    \PY{n}{min\PYZus{}samples\PYZus{}split}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{10}\PY{p}{,}   \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} splits only when enough samples are present}
    \PY{n}{min\PYZus{}samples\PYZus{}leaf}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{,}     \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} prevents very small leaf nodes}
    \PY{n}{random\PYZus{}state}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{42}
\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Train the model}
\PY{n}{dt\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{fit}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Make predictions}
\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred\PYZus{}dt} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{dt\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{predict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Evaluate model performance}
\PY{n}{mae\PYZus{}dt} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}absolute\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred\PYZus{}dt}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{mse\PYZus{}dt} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}squared\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred\PYZus{}dt}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{rmse\PYZus{}dt} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sqrt}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{mse\PYZus{}dt}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{r2\PYZus{}dt} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{r2\PYZus{}score}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred\PYZus{}dt}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{mape\PYZus{}dt} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{abs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred\PYZus{}dt}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mi}{100}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} MAPE}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Compute Adjusted R²}
\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{p} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}
\PY{n}{adjusted\PYZus{}r2\PYZus{}dt} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{r2\PYZus{}dt}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{p} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{✅ Pruned Decision Tree Performance (Test):}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAE: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{mae\PYZus{}dt}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MSE: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{mse\PYZus{}dt}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{RMSE: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{rmse\PYZus{}dt}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAPE: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{mape\PYZus{}dt}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{R²: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{r2\PYZus{}dt}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.4f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Adjusted R²: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{adjusted\PYZus{}r2\PYZus{}dt}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.4f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==============================}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ✅ Overfitting Check (Train vs Test)}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==============================}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Predictions on TRAIN data}
\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}pred\PYZus{}dt} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{dt\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{predict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{full\PYZus{}metrics}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}features}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{mae} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}absolute\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{mse} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}squared\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{rmse} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sqrt}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{mse}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{mape} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{abs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mi}{100}
    \PY{n}{r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{r2\PYZus{}score}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{adj\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{r2}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}features} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{mae}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{rmse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mape}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{r2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{adj\PYZus{}r2}

\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mae}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}rmse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mape}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}r2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{full\PYZus{}metrics}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}pred\PYZus{}dt}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{p}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mae}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}rmse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mape}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}r2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{full\PYZus{}metrics}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred\PYZus{}dt}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{p}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{================ TRAIN METRICS ================}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mae}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MSE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mse}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{RMSE       : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}rmse}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAPE       : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mape}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{R²         : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}r2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.4f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Adjusted R²: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.4f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{================ TEST METRICS =================}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mae}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MSE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mse}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{RMSE       : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}rmse}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAPE       : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mape}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{R²         : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}r2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.4f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Adjusted R²: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.4f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{==============================================}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Diagnose Overfitting}
\PY{k}{if} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ Model still slightly overfitting — increase regularization if needed.}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ Model is now well\PYZhy{}generalized (train and test performance close).}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Mean Absolute Error (MAE): }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{mae\PYZus{}dt}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Function to compute full metrics}
\PY{k}{def}\PY{+w}{ }\PY{n+nf}{full\PYZus{}metrics}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}features}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{mae} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}absolute\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{mse} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}squared\PYZus{}error}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{rmse} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sqrt}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{mse}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{mape} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{abs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mi}{100}
    \PY{n}{r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{r2\PYZus{}score}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}true}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{adj\PYZus{}r2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{r2}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{num\PYZus{}features} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{mae}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{rmse}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mape}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{r2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{adj\PYZus{}r2}

\PY{n}{p} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}train}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} number of predictors}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} TRAIN metrics}
\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mae\PYZus{}dt}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mse\PYZus{}dt}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}rmse\PYZus{}dt}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mape\PYZus{}dt}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}r2\PYZus{}dt}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2\PYZus{}dt} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{full\PYZus{}metrics}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}train\PYZus{}pred\PYZus{}dt}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{p}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} TEST metrics (same format)}
\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mae\PYZus{}dt}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mse\PYZus{}dt}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}rmse\PYZus{}dt}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mape\PYZus{}dt}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}r2\PYZus{}dt}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2\PYZus{}dt} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{full\PYZus{}metrics}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred\PYZus{}dt}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{p}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{================ TRAIN METRICS (Tuned Decision Tree) ================}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mae\PYZus{}dt}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MSE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mse\PYZus{}dt}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{RMSE       : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}rmse\PYZus{}dt}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAPE       : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}mape\PYZus{}dt}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{R²         : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}r2\PYZus{}dt}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.4f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Adjusted R²: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2\PYZus{}dt}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.4f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{================ TEST METRICS (Tuned Decision Tree) =================}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mae\PYZus{}dt}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MSE        : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mse\PYZus{}dt}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{RMSE       : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}rmse\PYZus{}dt}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{MAPE       : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}mape\PYZus{}dt}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{R²         : }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}r2\PYZus{}dt}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.4f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Adjusted R²: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}adj\PYZus{}r2\PYZus{}dt}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.4f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{=====================================================================}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Interpretation / Diagnosis}
\PY{k}{if} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}r2\PYZus{}dt} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}r2\PYZus{}dt} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.1}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o+ow}{and} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{train\PYZus{}rmse\PYZus{}dt} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}rmse\PYZus{}dt} \PY{o}{*} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.8}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ Model is OVERFITTING (Train performance much better than Test).}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{k}{elif} \PY{n}{train\PYZus{}r2\PYZus{}dt} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.3} \PY{o+ow}{and} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}r2\PYZus{}dt} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.3}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ Model is UNDERFITTING (Model too simple, not capturing patterns).}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ Model is WELL\PYZhy{}GENERALIZED (Train and Test performance are close).}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Actual}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Predicted}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}pred\PYZus{}dt}
\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{)}
